<script language="Javascript1.1" type="text/javascript">
    
  function dpCSSSetMinWidth() {
	var elem = document.getElementById("divsinglecolumnminwidth");
	if (elem) {
                dpCSSSetElemWidth(elem);
	}
  }
  
  function dpCSSSetElemWidth(elem) {
      if (elem) {
         var clientWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth ? document.documentElement.clientWidth : document.body.clientWidth;
         elem.runtimeStyle.width = (clientWidth < 920 ? '920px' : '100%' );
      }
  }
  
  if ( -1 != navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE") ) {
      window.onresize = dpCSSSetMinWidth;
  }

// =============================================================================
// Function Class: Show/Hide product promotions & special offers link
// =============================================================================

function showElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'visible';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'block';
    }
  }
}
function hideElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }
}
function showHideElement(h_id, div_id) {
  var hiddenTag = document.getElementById(h_id);
  if (hiddenTag) {
    showElement(div_id);
  } else {
    hideElement(div_id);
  }
}

    function findMatch(f){
	for(var attribution in attributionMap){
	    var i=0;
	    var attributionValue = attributionMap[attribution];
	    var files = attributionValue['files'];
	    while(files[i]){
		if(f.match(files[i])){
	            var exception={};
		    exception.attribution = attribution;
		    if(attributionValue.hasOwnProperty("logLevel")){
			exception.logLevel = attributionValue['logLevel'];	
		    }
		return exception;
           	}
		i++;
	    }
        }
	return null;
    }


    function dpOnErrorOverride(message, file, line, col, error){
     var matchingErrorFound = false;

                jsException.c =  "" + (col || "");

                jsException.args = arguments;
                if(window.ueLogError){
               	    window.ueLogError(jsException);
		    matchingErrorFound = true;
		    if(ue && ue.count){
		        ue.count("dpJavascriptAffectedErrors", (ue.count("dpJavascriptAffectedErrors") || 0) + 1);
		        ue.count("dpJSError" + jsException.attribution, (ue.count("dpJSError" + jsException.attribution) || 0) + 1);
		    }
	        }
            }
	}catch(exception){
	    if(window.ueLogError){
	        window.ueLogError(exception,{message: "dpOnErrorOverride: error occurred - ", logLevel:"FATAL"});
	    }
	}
    }
	if(!matchingErrorFound){ 
          old_error_handler.apply(this, arguments);
	}
        return false;
    }

      dpOnErrorOverride.skipTrace = 1;
      window.onerror = dpOnErrorOverride;
    })(window.onerror);

      function acrPopoverHover(e, h) {
        if(h) window.acrAsinHover = e;
        else if(window.acrAsinHover == e) window.acrAsinHover = null;
      }

  amznJQ.onReady('popover', function() {
    (function($) {
      if($.fn.acrPopover) return;
      var popoverConfig = {
        showOnHover:true,
        showCloseButton: true,
        width: null,
        location:'bottom',
        locationAlign:'left',
        locationOffset:[-20,0],
        paddingLeft: 15,
        paddingBottom: 5,
        paddingRight: 15,
        group: 'reviewsPopover',
        clone:false,
        hoverHideDelay:300
      };

      $.fn.acrPopover = function() {
          return this.each(function() {
            var $this = $(this);
            if(!$this.data('init') && typeof $this.amazonPopoverTrigger === 'function') {
              $this.data('init', 1);
              var getargs = $this.attr('getargs');
              var ajaxURL = '/gp/customer-reviews/common/du/displayHistoPopAjax.html?' +
                         '&ASIN=' + $this.attr('name') +
                         '&link=1' +
                         '&seeall=1' +
                         '&ref=' + $this.attr('ref') +
                         ((typeof getargs != 'undefined') ? ('&getargs=' + getargs) : '');
              var myConfig = $.extend(true, { destination: ajaxURL }, popoverConfig);
              $this.amazonPopoverTrigger(myConfig);

              var w = window.acrAsinHover;
              if(w && $(w).parents('.asinReviewsSummary').get(0) == this) {
                $this.trigger('mouseover.amzPopover');
                window.acrAsinHover = null;
              }
            }
        });
      };

      window.reviewHistPopoverConfig = popoverConfig;
      var jqInit = window.jQueryInitHistoPopovers = function(asin) {
        if (typeof $('.acr-popover[name=' + asin + ']').acrPopover === 'function') {
          $('.acr-popover[name=' + asin + ']').acrPopover();
        }
      };
      window.doInit_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onAjaxUpdate_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onCacheUpdate_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onCacheUpdateReselect_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;

      amznJQ.onCompletion('amznJQ.criticalFeature', function() {
          setTimeout(function() { amznJQ.declareAvailable('acrPopover'); }, 10);
      });
    })(jQuery);
  });
  amznJQ.onReady('acrPopover', function() {
    jQuery('.acr-popover,#searchTemplate .asinReviewsSummary').each(function() {
      if (typeof jQuery(this).acrPopover === 'function') {
        jQuery(this).acrPopover();
      }
    });
  });

if(gbEnableTwisterJS) {
    varBoxDiv = document.getElementById('variationBox');
    if (varBoxDiv) {varBoxDiv.style.display = 'none';}
    //Kill the innerHTML so non-js does not interfere.
    if (varBoxDiv) {varBoxDiv.innerHTML = '';}
    swatchDiv = document.getElementById('jsSwatches');
    if (swatchDiv) {swatchDiv.style.display = 'block';}

jQuery(document).bind("state_initialized", function() {
    if(gbEnableTwisterJS){         // Initialize goTwistervariations
        goTwisterVariations = new TwisterVariations(goSwatchVariationKeys, goDropdownVariationKeys);
        // Select Dimensions
        var varSelectedValues = DetailPage.StateController.getState()['selected_variation_values'];
        for (var varDim in varSelectedValues) {
            var preselect = (varDim == DetailPage.StateController.getState()['preselected_variation_dimension']);
            var varVal = preselect ? DetailPage.StateController.getState()['preselected_variation_index'] :varSelectedValues[varDim];
            if (varVal > -1) {
                var dropDownId = varDim;
                var swatchId = varDim + "_" + varVal;

                // Make initial selections
                if (document.getElementById(varDim) != null) {
                    var ddList = document.getElementById(varDim);
                    for (var i=1; ddList.options[i] != null; i++ ) {
                        if (ddList.options[i].value == varVal) {
                            ddList.options[i].selected = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    goTwisterVariations.onChangeDropdown(varDim,null,!preselect, true);
                } else {
                    var swatches = document.getElementById(swatchId);
                    if(swatches != null) {
                        swatches.className = 'swatchSelect';
                        goTwisterVariations.onClickSwatch(varDim, varVal, !preselect, true);
                    }
                }

                // Set Labels
                var selectedDiv = document.getElementById("selected_"+varDim);
                if(selectedDiv != null) {
                    if (DetailPage.StateController.getState()['variation_values'][varDim].length == 1) {
                        selectedDiv.innerHTML = '<b class=variationDefault>' + DetailPage.StateController.getState()['variation_display_labels'][varDim] + ':  </b>' + DetailPage.StateController.getState()['variation_values'][varDim][varVal] ;
                    } else {
                        selectedDiv.innerHTML = '<b class=variationDefault>' + DetailPage.StateController.getState()['variation_display_labels'][varDim] + ':  </b><b class=variationLabel>' + DetailPage.StateController.getState()['variation_values'][varDim][varVal] +  '</b>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
});

jQuery(document).bind('dpf_initialized', function() {

        goTwisterVariations.onLoad();
        if (DetailPage.StateController.getState()['is_shadow_singleton']) {
            goTwisterVariations.triggerEvent("select");
        }
    }
});

        window.SizingChart = function() {
            var isOpen = false;
            var open = function(link) {
                amznJQ.available("jQuery", function() {
                    var spinnerContent = "<div id='size-chart-spinner'><img src='"
                        + window.AmazonPopoverImages.snake + "'/></div>";
                    var url = jQuery(link).attr("href");
                    if (window.gOpenQuickview) {
                        window.gOpenQuickview.showSizingChart(url);
                    } else {
                        if(isOpen) return;
                        isOpen = true;
                        amznJQ.available("popover", function() {
                            var popover =  jQuery.AmazonPopover.displayPopover({
                                    literalContent: spinnerContent,
                                    location:"centered",
                                    width:800,
                                    zIndex:991,
                                    height:height,
                                    locationOffset:[0, -50],
                                    title:"",
                                    closeText:"",
                                    onHide: function() {
                                        isOpen = false;
                                    }
                                });

                            var iframeHeight = jQuery(window).height() - 180;
                            var height = Math.min(Math.max(iframeHeight,300), 700);

                            var fetchAjax = function() {
                                jQuery.ajax({
                                    url:url+"&height="+height,
                                    success: function(data) {
                                        data = data.replace(/\s*([^\s]*)\s*$/, "$1");
                                        if(data) {
                                            popover.find(".ap_content").html(data);
                                        } else {
                                            ajaxFailure();
                                        }
                                    },
                                    error: function() {
                                        ajaxFailure();
                                    }
                                });
                            };

                            var ajaxFailure = function() {
                                popover.find(".ap_content").html("<div id='size-chart-error'><p class='error-text'></p><p><a href='" + url + "'></a></p></div>");

                                popover.find("#size-chart-error a").click(function() {
                                    popover.find(".ap_content").html(spinnerContent);
                                    fetchAjax();
                                    return false;
                                });
                            };

                            fetchAjax();
                        });
                    }
                });

                return false;
            };

            return { open : open };
        }();

    if (this.initialized) { return; }   
    KDS.bbqRestriction.prototype.initialized = true;

    this.resASINs = resASINs;
    this.createAndCacheQDDs(resMaxQty,resPopTitle,resPopContent);

        }
      }; 
      DetailPageFramework.registerCallback('asin_select', 'kindle-availability-messaging', callback);

        instance.viewQDD(false);

  }; 
  
  KDS.bbqRestriction.prototype = { 
    preventTwisterOnloadBuyboxUpdate : function() { 
      DetailPageFramework.BuyBoxAdapter.prototype.updateDropdown = function(a,b,c) {};
    }, 
    createAndCacheQDDs : function(maxResQty,resPopTitle,resPopContent) {

      $("#quantityDropdownDiv").css("padding-bottom","22px").css("margin-top","2px");
      $("#quantityDropdownDiv span").css('position','absolute').css("left","49px"); 

      this.unResQDD = $("#quantityDropdownDiv #quantity")
                      .css('position','absolute').css("left","117px"); 
      this.resQDD = $('<select></select>').append((function () { 
        var options = "";
        for (var i = 1; i <= maxResQty; i++) { 
          options += '<option value="'+i+'">'+i+'</option>';
        } 
        return options;
      })())
      .css('position','absolute').css("visibility", "hidden").css("left","117px");

      if($.browser.msie) { 
        $("#quantityDropdownDiv span").css("margin-top","3px"); 
        this.unResQDD.css("margin-top","-2px"); 
        this.resQDD.css("margin-top","-2px"); 
      } else { 
        this.unResQDD.css("margin-top","0px"); 
        this.resQDD.css("margin-top","0px"); 
      } 

      var lastRowVal = (maxResQty+1)+"+";       
      var lastRow = $('<option value="' + lastRowVal + '" id="lastQuantityOption">'+lastRowVal+'</option>');

      amznJQ.onReady('popover', function() { 
        $(document).ready(function() { 
          lastRow.amazonPopoverTrigger({ 
            hoverShowDelay: 200, 
            hoverHideDelay: 200, 
            width: 502, 
            showCloseButton: true, 
            literalContent: resPopContent, 
            title: resPopTitle, 
            skin: "default",  
            locationElement: "#quantityDropdownDiv select", 
            location: "left", 
            closeEventExclude: "CLICK_TRIGGER" 
          }); 
        }); 
      }); 

      var resQDDPointer = this.resQDD;
      this.resQDD.append(lastRow).change(function() {  
        if (resQDDPointer.val() == lastRowVal) {
          lastRow.trigger("click"); 
          resQDDPointer.children("option[value=1]").attr('selected','selected'); 
        } 
      });

      $("#quantityDropdownDiv").append(this.resQDD); 
    },
    viewQDD : function(restricted) { 
      var toHide = this.resQDD;
      var toShow = this.unResQDD;

      if (restricted) { 
        toHide = this.unResQDD;
        toShow = this.resQDD;
      }       

      toHide.attr("id","").attr("name","").css("visibility", "hidden"); 
      toShow.attr("id","quantity").attr("name","quantity").css("visibility", "visible");
      toShow.children("option[value=1]").attr('selected','selected'); 
    }
  };   
  amznJQ.declareAvailable("bbqRestrictionJS");
})(jQuery);
}); 


</script>

amznJQ.available('jQuery', function() {
(function ($) {
    $('.kindle-feature-bullets-toggle').click(function () {
        var toggleId = $(this).attr('id'),
            moreElement = $('#kindle-feature-bullets-atf-more'),
            moreToggleClass = 'kindle-feature-bullets-show-more';

        if (toggleId === moreToggleClass) {
            moreElement.show();
            $(this).hide();
        } else {
            moreElement.hide();
            $('#' + moreToggleClass).show();
        }
    });

           <td style="width:100%; " class="kmd-standard-padding kmd-last-col"> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Wi-Fi</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">A Kindle Paperwhite or Kindle Voyage with Wi-Fi is a great choice if you already have a high-speed internet connection and wireless router set up in your home. If you do not have Wi-Fi set up at home, a 3G model may be a better option&#x2014;3G connectivity lets you download books anytime, anywhere.</p> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Wi-Fi + free 3G</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body kmd-paragraph-last">A model with Wi-Fi + free 3G is the easiest option because there is no wireless setup&#x2014;you are ready to shop, purchase, and read right out of the box. Built-in free 3G connectivity uses the same wireless signals that cell phones use, but there are no monthly fees or commitments&#x2014;Amazon pays for 3G wireless connectivity. The added convenience of 3G enables you to download books anytime, anywhere, without having to find a Wi-Fi hotspot connection. Your Kindle may use wireless connectivity to make other services available, such as wireless delivery of personal documents, which may require an additional charge. For more information, see <a href="/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=200506200" target="_blank">Wireless Terms and Conditions</a> <br><br> With wireless coverage in over 100 countries and territories, 3G lets you download books anytime, anywhere, whether you're relaxing on a beach, halfway through a hike, or waiting on the tarmac. <a href="http://client0.cellmaps.com/viewer.html?cov=1" target="_blank">Check 3G coverage area</a> <br><br> For U.S. customers traveling abroad, additional charges apply for wireless delivery of periodical subscriptions. To avoid any charges, you can always use a Wi-Fi connection or download items via your computer and transfer them to your Kindle using USB. <br><br> Some books may not be eligible for download over 3G wireless, including promotional content or where indicated on a book detail page. </p> </td>

           <td style="width:50%; " class="kmd-standard-padding "> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Customize to your language</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">Kindle Voyage can be used in English, Spanish, Brazilian Portuguese, French, German, Italian, Japanese, Russian, Dutch, and Simplified Chinese. You can easily select the language that you are most comfortable with, and enjoy instant dictionary lookups in any of these languages.</p> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Read books in other languages</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">Kindle Voyage supports the display of non-Latin characters, so you can read books and documents in your favorite language, including enhanced support for Japanese and Chinese (Simplified and Traditional). Kindle Voyage also displays Korean, Cyrillic, Latin, and Greek scripts, and provides free access to several international dictionaries.</p> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Follow along with page numbers</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">We match the pages of a Kindle book to the text in a print book to identify the corresponding page number. Easily reference and cite passages or read alongside others in a book club or class.</p> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">WebKit-based browser</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body kmd-paragraph-last">Kindle Voyage has an experimental web browser based on WebKit. It's easy to find the information you're looking for right from your Kindle Voyage. Kindle Voyage enables you to connect to the Kindle Store and access Wikipedia, all over Wi-Fi.</p> </td>
           <td style="width:50%;" class="kmd-standard-padding kmd-last-col"> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Never lose a book</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">We automatically back up your entire Kindle library free in the cloud so there's never a worry about losing your books. Re-download wirelessly anytime for free.</p> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Carry and read personal documents</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">Email documents&#x2014;including Word, PDF, and more&#x2014;directly to your Kindle and read them in Kindle format. You can also send documents to Kindle Voyage using <a target="_blank" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/sendtokindle">Send to Kindle</a>.</p> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Get special offers</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">Love deals? You'll receive special offers and sponsored screensavers directly on your Kindle Voyage. Offers display on the Kindle Voyage screensaver and on the bottom of the home screen while not in use&#x2014;they don't interrupt reading.</p> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Read children?s books and comics</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body ">Kindle Voyage supports children's books with Kindle Text Pop-Up, and comic books with Kindle Panel View which allows you to read a comic book panel by panel.</p> <h4 class="kmd-paragraph-title">Organize your library</h4> <p class="kmd-text-paragraph-body kmd-paragraph-last">Organize your Kindle library into customized collections, or categories, to easily access any book you are looking for. You can add an item to multiple collections to make organizing and finding titles even easier.</p> </td> 
          </tr>

           <span class="swSprite s_star_5_0 " title="5.0 out of 5 stars"><span>5.0 out of 5 stars</span></span> 
           <a href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R3KVJS35XJVP8B" class="txtlarge gl3 gr4 reviewTitle valignMiddle"><strong>The state of the art e-ink reader but is it worth the money to upgrade</strong></a>
           <span class="gry valignMiddle"> <span class="inlineblock txtsmall">October 22, 2014</span> </span>
          </div> 
          <div class="mt4 ath">
           <span class="gr10"> <span class="txtsmall"><span class="gry">By</span> <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A1E1LEVQ9VQNK" class="noTextDecoration">J. Chambers</a></span> </span>

          <div class="mt9 reviewText"> 
           <div class="fl gr19">

           <div class="drkgry"> 
            <span class="MHRHead">Although I've owned almost every model of Kindle ebook readers since the 2nd generation Kindle that I bought in 2009, I had to think hard about ordering the new Voyage. I was very happy with my Paperwhite (the 2nd generation that was released in the fall of 2013), and as much as I wanted to try the Voyage, I wasn't sure I wanted to spend $199 on one. It became a moot point, though, when my wife ordered the Voyage, saying it was her early Christmas present to me. Now that I've had time to use the Voyage, I have to say I'm impressed. With hardware features like a 300 ppi display, LEDs that automatically adjust the screen brightness depending on the ambient lighting, and the user's choice of a touchscreen or sensors acting like buttons to turn pages, the Voyage is hands down the state-of-the-art e-ink ebook reader. At the end of my review, I'll give my opinion on whether it's worth upgrading from your current ebook reader.<br><br>When I received the Voyage, the setup was quick (although you do have to go through a brief tutorial), and after downloading a few of my books from the Amazon Cloud and adjusting a few settings, the Voyage was ready to go. Here's a brief comparison of the Voyage and the Paperwhite:<br><br>Voyage<br>---------<br>Size: 6.4"x4.5"x0.30"<br>Weight (wi-fi version): 6.3 ounces<br>Display: 6" diagonal, 300 pixels per inch, 16-level grayscale, LED frontlit<br>Storage memory: 4GB<br>Page turns: Touchscreen plus PagePress<br>Display lighting: Adaptive light sensor (automatic) plus manual adjustment<br><br>Paperwhite<br>-------------<br>Size: 6.7"x4.6"x0.36"<br>Weight (wi-fi version): 7.</span>
            <span class="MHRRest" style="display:none">3 ounces<br>Display: 6" diagonal, 212 pixels per inch, 16-level grayscale, LED frontlit<br>Storage memory: 4GB (for the Paperwhites currently being sold)<br>Page turns: Touchscreen<br>Display lighting: Manually adjustable front-lighting<br><br>So the Voyage weighs an ounce less than the Paperwhite, and it's slightly smaller. Those are not substantial differences, but it might make a difference if you hand-hold your ebook reader for long periods of time. The higher resolution does make a difference, however, especially if you read many books with illustrations or photographs. I've been reading most illustrated books on my Kindle Fire, but with the increased resolution, I may read them on the Voyage now. And the Voyage's 300ppi resolution compared to the Paperwhite's 212ppi definitely makes a difference in viewing. Even the smallest font size is very sharp, although I prefer a slightly larger font for reading.<br><br>Besides the smaller size, the Voyage has some other obvious differences from the Paperwhite. The shell is made of magnesium instead of plastic. The capacitive touch screen is made of hardened glass instead of a plastic-like material. The Kindles have always been pretty resistant to damage if they were dropped. (Remember the videos Amazon used to show to demonstrate that?) The change in materials should make the Voyage even more resistant to damage. The location of the power button has moved from the bottom of the case to the rear of the case, at the top right, but if you're using a cover that activates the Voyage's Auto Wake function, you'll seldom need to touch the power button. The micro-USB charging port remains at the bottom.<br><br>One of the most significant new hardware features on the voyage are the pressure-sensitive page turn sensors. The last few Kindle models did away with raised buttons in favor of touchscreen controls. I prefer the touchscreen, but Amazon has obviously listened to Kindle users who miss the buttons, so they're back, but they're in a new flush, pressure-sensitive design that Amazon calls PagePress. The PagePress sensors are located on the sides of the bezel (the frame around the screen), which in the Voyage is flush with the screen, whereas in the Paperwhite, the bezel is raised about a millimeter above the screen. (This makes it less likely for sand or dust to get trapped along the edges of the screen.) The PagePress sensors are located on both sides of the bezel, so they're ambidextrous (thank you from all of us southpaws). Press the long vertical line on either side of the bezel to turn the page, and the dot sitting above it to flip back one page. You'll feel a slight vibration to confirm that you've pressed the sensor. The amount of vibration and the sensor's sensitivity can be adjusted in the settings. If you prefer touchscreen controls, the PagePress sensors can be turned off so you don't accidentally flip pages. After seeing how they worked (and they do work well), I turned them off. One thought: If you're reading on the Voyage in a darkened room, you can see the screen just fine, but you can't see the PagePress sensors, especially the little dots for returning to the previous page. It might have been better if they had made little bumps for some tactile feedback to your fingers.<br><br>Another new hardware feature that I like is the Voyage's new adaptive lighting that automatically adjusts the brightness of the screen depending on the lighting of your surroundings. You can turn it off and adjust the brightness manually (like the Paperwhite) if you want to, but I tried it in several lighting conditions, and it works pretty well. When reading the Voyage in the dark, you can use the Nightlight feature to gradually reduce the screen brightness over time as your eyes adjust. To enable Nightlight, go to Settings, Device Options, then Screen Light. With my Paperwhite 1, I could see noticeable shadows across the bottom of the screen from the lighting; it was much less noticeable on my Paperwhite 2, but the lighting appears to be perfectly uniform on the Voyage. Like all of the Kindles, the Voyage's display is very readable outdoors even in bright sunlight that makes backlit tablets and phones almost impossible to read.<br><br>The storage memory in the Voyage is 4GB, the most memory that Amazon has ever put in a new Kindle. After accounting for the operating system, there's about 3GB available for books. Amazon says that's enough for thousands of books. Even with books that have illustrations and graphics, 3GB will hold a lot of books. Personally, I doubt if I've ever had more than a hundred books on a Kindle. With every book that you purchased from Amazon being stored in the Cloud, there's really not much need to store thousands of books on a Kindle, but the memory is available if you need it.<br><br>I haven't had the Voyage long enough to get a feel for the battery life. According to Amazon, a full charge will last up to six weeks, based on a half hour of reading per day with wireless off and the light setting at 10 (the maximum is 24). Battery life will vary based on the illumination setting and wireless usage. I've always used my Kindles a lot, and since the Voyage uses a tiny graphic to show the remaining charge instead of a digital readout, I'll keep on recharging it about every two weeks to keep the battery from going dead.<br><br>The Voyage's software is pretty much the same as the Paperwhite's. The Voyage retains what I thought was the most useful new software feature of the Paperwhite - Page Flip. It's the digital equivalent of putting a finger between pages of a paper book while flipping back (or forward) to see other pages. To turn on Page Flip, swipe up from the bottom of the screen, and you'll see a pop-up of the page you're on. You can then go back or forward to find whatever it is you're looking for. When you're done, tap the "X" in the upper right of the pop-up, and it goes away. This is a really useful feature, although using the search function is often an easier way to find things.<br><br>In other software features, the Voyage includes full Goodreads integration, which was added later to the Paperwhite. And like the Paperwhite, the Voyage has a web browser that enables it to look up words on Wikipedia when you press and hold on the word. In a pinch, you can use it as a general web browser, but keep in mind that it's fairly slow and it's in grayscale. In other words, it's clunky.<br><br>Note that a USB charging cable is included in the box, but you'll need to provide your own AC charger. Amazon sells a 5V/1A charger (<a href="http://www.amazon.com/Amazon-Kindle-USB-Power-Adapter/dp/B00BGIQS1A">Amazon Kindle 5W USB Power Adapter</a>), but there are tons of third-party chargers sold, with many of them costing less than Amazon's. Actually, your cellphone or tablet charger will work fine in most cases. You can also recharge the Voyage's battery from a USB port, but it may take longer.<br><br>I highly recommend a cover to protect the screen and to make it easier to hand-hold the Voyage. If you do get a cover, get one that supports the Voyage's Auto Wake function that puts the Voyage to sleep when you close the cover and wakes it when you open the cover. My favorites are the very thin, lightweight covers that fold back for one-handed reading.<br><br>I purchased the Kindle Voyage with wi-fi only and with the special offers. Frankly, I don't think most people really need 3G for an ebook reader. Wi-fi is so available in most locations nowadays that it doesn't seem worth the extra cost to get a 3G ebook reader. If you're traveling to a location that doesn't have wi-fi, just download the books you want to read before you leave home. If you do get the 3G option, note that AT&amp;T provides the connection for Amazon's Whispernet service, so you should be able to receive a signal anywhere within AT&amp;T's coverage area. About the special offers, you get used to them so quickly that you hardly notice them. And they're not intrusive - they don't pop up while you're reading - they only show on the lock screen and at the bottom half-inch of your book listings, and you swipe them away in a second. My advice: Save your $20 and get the special offers. And a lot of the special offers are worth seeing anyway.<br><br>Okay, the bottom line: Is the Voyage worth $199? In my opinion, if you're perfectly happy with your Paperwhite or other Kindle, there's no compelling reason to upgrade at this time. On the other hand, if you're a techno-geek or someone who reads a lot of books and insists on having the latest and greatest e-ink reader, there's nothing else on the market that even comes close to the technology of the Voyage, so go for it. If you're one of those folks who reads a lot but has resisted buying an ebook reader, the Voyage may be for you. With your choice of swiping or pushing buttons to turn pages, you get the best of both worlds. And as pricy as the Voyage is, it's only half the cost of the original 2007 Kindle, which had almost none of the bells and whistles the Voyage has (but it did have a speaker and headphone jack for the text-to-speech feature, which the newer Kindles, including the Voyage, lack). Another factor you might consider is that Amazon recently released a new 6" Kindle Fire HD tablet for under a hundred dollars. The Kindle Fires are all-purpose color tablets with hi-res displays that are fine for reading ebooks, although many people say they can't read for long on a backlit tablet without getting eyestrain.<br><br>Based on the Voyage's features and its performance, it's a solid 5 stars in my opinion, but honestly, it's a lot of money, considering that the Paperwhite is much less expensive and is a great ebook reader in its own right.</span> 
            <a href="http://www.amazon.com/High-Resolution-Display-Adaptive-PagePress-Sensors/product-reviews/B00IOY8XWQ" class="MHRExpandLink readMoreLink">Read more &#x203a;</a>

          <div class="mt9 reviewText"> 
           <div class="drkgry"> 
            <span class="MHRHead">I've got mixed feelings on this one, unfortunately. This review is coming from a kindle enthusiast who has owned or used nearly every variation of the device since the 1st generation.<br><br>Size &amp; Weight<br>---<br>It's noticeably smaller and lighter than the Paperwhite. When I saw the specs it didn't really strike me as something that would make much difference to me, but in real life it's actually great. The Voyage fits into a few of my coat pockets that the Paperwhite was just a little too big to fit into.<br><br>Origami Cover<br>---<br>I know there's a separate product page for the origami cover, but it's worth mentioning here as it is the "official" cover. The origami cover is ugly and I was skeptical, but I actually love it. It's weird because it opens by flipping over the top like a notepad. This actually makes it more comfortable to hold when the cover is open, in my opinion. It's hard to describe, but there are a lot more ways to hold the Voyage when it's attached to this cover, and just generally is more comfortable to use. The origami part of the case works great as well... it stands vertically or horizontally (if you're laying down and reading, this is amazing).<br><br>The other great new thing about this case is that the Voyage attaches to it magnetically. It attaches and detaches very easily, unlike the Paperwhite which seemed to be nearly permanently attached to the standard case. This is great because if you decide you want to read the device and appreciate how light/thin it is without a case attached, it's super easy to take it out.<br><br>It's pricey but worth it.<br><br>PagePress<br>---<br>One of the new features is PagePress, which has sensors on the outer edge of the device that you can squeeze to turn pages.</span>
            <span class="MHRRest" style="display:none"> The device lets you adjust the sensitivity between low/med/high -- by default it's set to medium. I found medium to require squeezing way too hard, what felt unnatural and more than any button would or should require to advance to the next page. I adjusted it to "low" and it works perfectly now. Thumb rests on the sensor, and a gentle squeeze advances the page, and haptic feedback (a tiny vibration/buzz) is there to give you a tactile response that the so-called button was pressed. The haptic feedback can be adjusted (low/med/high)or disabled as well. It doesn't trigger accidentally like I feared it might, and I actually really like it.<br><br>Auto Brightness<br>---<br>The device now has a light sensor in the top left corner that is supposed to detect ambient light levels and adjust the brightness of the Kindle accordingly. I've had very mixed results with this. First, auto brightness is disabled on the device by default -- which seems odd given that it's one of the key new features of the device. The auto brightness worked very briefly when I first got the device, but it always seemed to be a little off from how I would like the screen to look. In lit rooms, it tended to be a little on the darker side, and in dark rooms it was too bright.<br><br>Well, shortly after using the Voyage the auto brightness quit working altogether. I restarted the device a few times with no luck. After contacting support, they asked me to proceed with a factory reset. It's worked again since then, but doesn't leave me with a ton of confidence since it started acting up so quickly after getting the device.<br><br>Screen<br>---<br>I've seen the reports online of users who have a "two toned" screen -- blueish on the bottom, yellowish on the top. I'm afraid to say that I have experienced this as well. Spending upwards of $200 for a luxury ereader, it's really surprising and disappointing that they haven't got this figured out by now -- this is supposed to be a premium device and it's the 3rd generation frontlit reader for amazon. This is reminiscent of the Paperwhite V1 launch with all of the splotchy lighting -- while it was a huge leap over the prior generation, you expect something like this to work perfectly. It doesn't.<br><br>The Paperwhite V1 had splotchy lighting, Paperwhite V2 was supposed to have "improved" lighting -- which it did, but still wasn't perfect (mine still had some bright spots)... but to be honest, the lighting on my Paperwhite V2 looks better and more consistent than the Voyage. It's unfortunate that this is a step back. I hope this isn't a widespread issue, but I fear that it is after seeing numerous users on other forums posting about it and sharing pictures of their device. It'll be a shame if the only upgrade next year will be a Voyage V2 with "improved lighting", just like what happened with the Paperwhite. I'll be more skeptical about being an early adopter next time.<br><br>Aside from the uneven lighting, which I can't decide how distracting it is, the contrast and picture quality of the screen is outstanding. When I compare the text from my Paperwhite V2 to the Voyage side-by-side, the text on the Paperwhite almost looks blurry -- which I wouldn't have believed until I saw it myself.<br><br>In conclusion, my favorite things about the Voyage are how much more comfortable it is to use (the origami cover offering more ways to hold/use the device, the pagepress sensor working great), the quality of the screen is outstanding, but the uneven lighting and flakey auto brightness are leaving me disappointed. I'm not sure if these were rushed out too quickly or if Amazon has poor quality control, but either way it's unacceptable.</span>

          <div class="gry txtsmall hlp">
           1,939 of 2,011 people found the following review helpful

          <div class="clearboth"></div> 
          <div class="mt4 ttl">
           <span class="swSprite s_star_5_0 " title="5.0 out of 5 stars"><span>5.0 out of 5 stars</span></span> 
           <a href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R2BH23NJ15H5CG" class="txtlarge gl3 gr4 reviewTitle valignMiddle"><strong>I was very happy with my Paperwhite and would not have bought this ...</strong></a>
           <span class="gry valignMiddle"> <span class="inlineblock txtsmall">October 23, 2014</span> </span>
          </div> 
          <div class="mt4 ath">
           <span class="gr10"> <span class="txtsmall"><span class="gry">By</span> <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A1ZST491WTFMO9" class="noTextDecoration">K.E. Fuhrmann</a></span> </span> 
          </div> 
          <div class="txtsmall mt4 fvavp">
           <span class="inlineblock formatVariation"> <span class="gr3 gry formatKey">Configuration:</span><span class="formatValue">Without Special Offers</span><span class="gl7 gr7 gry">|</span></span>
           <span class="inlineblock formatVariation"> <span class="gr3 gry formatKey">Connectivity Technology:</span><span class="formatValue">Wi-Fi Only</span><span class="gl7 gr7 gry">|</span></span>
           <span class="inlineblock avpOrVine"><span class="orange strong avp">Verified Purchase</span></span>
          </div> 
          <div class="mt9 reviewText"> 
           <div class="drkgry"> 
            <span class="MHRHead">Since other people have gone into detail on the device, I will answer only the burning questions I had before I received mine. I was very happy with my Paperwhite and would not have bought this had mine not been stolen/lost (not sure which). My husband still has his Paperwhite, so I was able to compare them side by side.<br><br>CAN I USE THE WALL CHARGER FROM MY PAPERWHITE TO CHARGE THE VOYAGE?<br><br>Yes.<br><br>CAN PRESSING THE PAGE TURNERS CAUSE REPETITIVE USE ISSUES?<br><br>I don't think so. You can turn down the pressure it needs (which is very slight) or you can turn it off completely and turn pages with a tap. It's actually nice to have both options.<br><br>CAN YOU SEE WHERE TO TURN THE PAGES IN THE DARK?<br><br>No. You can guess where the page forward area is, but the page back is a dot, so guessing would be difficult. But you can still tap to turn pages. Using a cover helps, as the edge of the cover would be right over the dot.<br><br>DOES THE FEEDBACK BUZZ ANNOY YOU WHEN YOU TURN PAGES?<br><br>I think it does take a little getting used to, but you can turn it down, and I think I will not notice it after a while. (There's no sound; it's purely tactile.) [Months later: It's not distracting; you forget about it.]<br><br>IS THE ADJUSTABLE LIGHT NICE?<br><br>I still do it manually. It doesn't adjust the way I'd like it to. Not as bright in good light as I'd like, and not as dim while my husband is sleeping next to me. Note that if you want to use the "night light," you have to set that separately from Auto Adjust. Settings/Device Options/Screen Light. I'm not actually sure that the night light is working. It was at 18 when I turned off the light (this is quite bright), and I checked it about 10 minutes later, and it was at 17.</span>
            <span class="MHRRest" style="display:none"> My eyes adjust a lot faster than that. I turned it down manually to about 7.<br><br>CAN I USE THE COVER/CASE FROM MY PAPERWHITE FOR THE VOYAGE?<br><br>I had a Fintie, and I tried it. The entire reading area was still completely visible, but there was about 1/4" of extra space above and I couldn't access the power button. You need to access the power button in the back to wake it out of screen saver mode, and you'd have to take it out of the cover to do that. It would protect it, though, in a suitcase while you're traveling. I ended up buying another Fintie for the Voyage and I'm very happy with it.<br><br>IS THE CRISPNESS OF THE TEXT AND WHITENESS OF THE BACKGROUND BETTER THAN THE PAPERWHITE?<br><br>It is, but I don't think I would have noticed if I did not have them side by side. If you have issues with your eyes, though, you will probably find it helps. [Months later: I'm enjoying the brighter light and slightly crisper text. Though I would still buy a Paperwhite again if my Voyage disappeared, I think the little shadow at the bottom of the PW would bug me now.]<br><br>ANY ISSUES?<br><br>I do not have any of the page hue issues that others have. The screen is uniformly white.<br><br>At first, I was having a problem with the page turners being located at just the spot where I like to hold the device. It took a while to find a comfortable way to hold it consistently. My thumb kept wanting to move to that spot, causing me to inadvertently change pages. Using a cover helps.<br><br>BOOKS IN THE PUBLIC DOMAIN AND A COUPLE OF TIPS<br><br>There is a way to easily download public domain books from Project Gutenberg on your Kindle by using the experimental browser. Open the browser on your Kindle (in the main menu) and type in the URL: www.freekindlebooks.org This will open a link to what's known as the Magic Catalog. When you have downloaded the catalog, it will appear on your home page and will look like a book. When you open it, you will see it is a listing of all the books in Project Gutenberg, and all these books are linked to their website. You can search for something (like, say, Peter Pan), and download it from the catalog right onto your device without having to connect to a computer. Very nifty. This can be done on any Kindle, not just the Voyage. Be sure to use the domain name ORG, not COM. freekindlebooks.com is something completely different.<br><br>You can also download books from the mobile site: m.gutenberg.org. But you would have to open the browser each time, as opposed to the Magic Catalog, where the links are already there.<br><br>Tips:<br><br>Know that you can turn off the public notes and highlights that appear in your book, and you can also turn off the "Recommended Content" that appears on the bottom of your home page.<br><br>Conclusion:<br><br>If you are happy with your Paperwhite, I would recommend sticking with it. Only buy the Voyage if you have money to throw around and like buying all the latest gadgets. The Voyage is fabulous, but the Paperwhite is perfectly fine. If you have a keyboard Kindle, the Paperwhite is much better than what you have in terms of clarity, brightness and readability.<br><br>Leave me a comment if you need further instructions on anything.</span>

   <script>

if (!window.KDS) { window.KDS = {}; }

amznJQ.available('jQuery', function() {
if (typeof KDS.bbqRestriction !== "undefined") { return; }  

(function($){
  KDS.bbqRestriction = function(resPopTitle,resPopContent,resMaxQty,resASINs) {  
    if (this.initialized) { return; }   
    KDS.bbqRestriction.prototype.initialized = true;

    this.resASINs = resASINs;
    this.createAndCacheQDDs(resMaxQty,resPopTitle,resPopContent);    
  
    var instance = this;
    if (typeof DetailPageFramework != 'undefined' && DetailPageFramework.registerCallback) {
      var callback = function() { 
        if (instance.resASINs[DetailPage.StateController.getState()['current_asin']]) {
          instance.viewQDD(true); 
        } else {
          instance.viewQDD(false); 
        }
      }; 
      DetailPageFramework.registerCallback('asin_select', 'kindle-availability-messaging', callback);
      this.preventTwisterOnloadBuyboxUpdate(); 
      callback(); 
    } else {
      if (instance.resASINs[$('#ASIN').val()]){ 
        instance.viewQDD(true); 
      } else { 
        instance.viewQDD(false); 
      } 
    }

  }; 
  
  KDS.bbqRestriction.prototype = { 
    preventTwisterOnloadBuyboxUpdate : function() { 
      DetailPageFramework.BuyBoxAdapter.prototype.updateDropdown = function(a,b,c) {};
    }, 
    createAndCacheQDDs : function(maxResQty,resPopTitle,resPopContent) {

      $("#quantityDropdownDiv").css("padding-bottom","22px").css("margin-top","2px");
      $("#quantityDropdownDiv span").css('position','absolute').css("left","49px"); 

      this.unResQDD = $("#quantityDropdownDiv #quantity")
                      .css('position','absolute').css("left","117px"); 
      this.resQDD = $('<select></select>').append((function () { 
        var options = "";
        for (var i = 1; i <= maxResQty; i++) { 
          options += '<option value="'+i+'">'+i+'</option>';
        } 
        return options;
      })())
      .css('position','absolute').css("visibility", "hidden").css("left","117px");

      if($.browser.msie) { 
        $("#quantityDropdownDiv span").css("margin-top","3px"); 
        this.unResQDD.css("margin-top","-2px"); 
        this.resQDD.css("margin-top","-2px"); 
      } else { 
        this.unResQDD.css("margin-top","0px"); 
        this.resQDD.css("margin-top","0px"); 
      } 

      var lastRowVal = (maxResQty+1)+"+";       
      var lastRow = $('<option value="' + lastRowVal + '" id="lastQuantityOption">'+lastRowVal+'</option>');

      amznJQ.onReady('popover', function() { 
        $(document).ready(function() { 
          lastRow.amazonPopoverTrigger({ 
            hoverShowDelay: 200, 
            hoverHideDelay: 200, 
            width: 502, 
            showCloseButton: true, 
            literalContent: resPopContent, 
            title: resPopTitle, 
            skin: "default",  
            locationElement: "#quantityDropdownDiv select", 
            location: "left", 
            closeEventExclude: "CLICK_TRIGGER" 
          }); 
        }); 
      }); 

      var resQDDPointer = this.resQDD;
      this.resQDD.append(lastRow).change(function() {  
        if (resQDDPointer.val() == lastRowVal) {
          lastRow.trigger("click"); 
          resQDDPointer.children("option[value=1]").attr('selected','selected'); 
        } 
      });

      $("#quantityDropdownDiv").append(this.resQDD); 
    },
    viewQDD : function(restricted) { 
      var toHide = this.resQDD;
      var toShow = this.unResQDD;

      if (restricted) { 
        toHide = this.unResQDD;
        toShow = this.resQDD;
      }       

      toHide.attr("id","").attr("name","").css("visibility", "hidden"); 
      toShow.attr("id","quantity").attr("name","quantity").css("visibility", "visible");
      toShow.children("option[value=1]").attr('selected','selected'); 
    }
  };   
  amznJQ.declareAvailable("bbqRestrictionJS");
})(jQuery);
}); 


</script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
amznJQ.onReady('kindleDeviceJS', function() {
  BBPopover.sessionId = '000-0000000-0000000';
  var refTag = 'kin3w_ddp_pop7';
  var learnMoreLink = jQuery("#bb_lm_B00BGIQS1A").attr("href");
  if ( learnMoreLink ) {
    var refTagPattern = /ref=\w*/;
    refTag = refTagPattern.exec( learnMoreLink );
    refTag = new String(refTag).substr( 4 ); 
  }

  BBPopover.refTag['B00BGIQS1A'] = refTag;
  BBPopover.registerDynamicPopover( 'B00BGIQS1A', function() {

    BBPopover.selectedAsin['B00BGIQS1A'] = 'B00BGIQS1A';
    BBPopover.displayedAsin['B00BGIQS1A'] = 'B00BGIQS1A';
    BBPopover.originalAsin['B00BGIQS1A'] = 'B00BGIQS1A';

    jQuery.ajax({
      cache: false,
      data: {
        "asin": "B00BGIQS1A",
        "asinCSVList" : "",
        "sId" : BBPopover.sessionId,
        "baseRef" : BBPopover.refTag['B00BGIQS1A'],
        "isFirstLoad" : 1,
        "bundlePriceOverride" : ""
      },
      dataType: "json",
      success: function(data, status) {
        if ( data && data.error == 0 ) {
          for ( var key in data ) {
            if ( key == "error" ) {
              continue;
            }
            BBPopover.asinCache[key] = data[key];
            jQuery('#bb_extra_B00BGIQS1A').children('.popoverLoading').css('display','none');
            BBPopover.doUpdate( 'B00BGIQS1A', key, 1 );
            /* Pull in the image size from its parent object setting */
            var imgParam = jQuery('#bb_extra_feature_B00BGIQS1A_productImage').css('height');
            jQuery('#bb_extra_feature_B00BGIQS1A_productImage img').css('height',imgParam);
            /* Display all product info after aloading*/
            jQuery('#bb_extra_B00BGIQS1A').children('.popoverLoaded').css('display','block');
          }
        }
      },
      type: "GET",
      url: "/gp/digital/fiona/ajax/buyBoxTwister/ref=" + BBPopover.refTag['B00BGIQS1A'] + "_bbpfl"
    });
  });
});
</script>

        "sId" : BBPopover.sessionId,

            BBPopover.doUpdate( 'B00QLEI0B0', key, 1 );

   <script type="text/javascript">
var eventObj; // to make global event accessible in Firefox
amznJQ.onReady('popover', function() {
    amznJQ.onReady('kindleDeviceJS', function() {
	    var allAsins = new Array();
                allAsins.push('B00BGIQS1A');
                allAsins.push('B00J7WJE8G');
    var refTag = '';
    var asinsToShow = new Array();

    var intlPopover = {};
    intlPopover.shouldAutocheck = false;

intlPopover.onShow = function onShow(allAsins, event)  {
        asinsToShow = [];	
	for (var i=0; i<allAsins.length;i++) {           
	    var asin = allAsins[i];
	    var checkbox = jQuery("#bb_chk_" + asin);
            var shown = jQuery("#tracc_"+asin).css('display');
            var asinHtmlId = "#intl_pop_" + asin;
            jQuery(asinHtmlId).hide(); //make all asin hidden as start

	    // If there's no corresponding checkbox in the buy box, the ASIN won't show up in interstitial
	    if (checkbox.length > 0 && !checkbox.is(':checked') && shown != 'none') {
		asinsToShow.push(asin);
	    }
	}
	
	if (asinsToShow.length == 0) {
	    jQuery(intlPopover.buttonParent).removeAmazonPopoverTrigger();
	} else {

	    if (asinsToShow.length == 1) {
		var asin = asinsToShow[0];

		// switch to the single-asin ATC layout
	        jQuery("#intl_pop_multi_atc").hide();
		jQuery("#intl_pop_single_atc").show();
		jQuery('.intl_pop_chk_atc').hide();
	    }
            
            for (var i=0; i<asinsToShow.length; i++) {

		var asin = asinsToShow[i];
		var asinHtmlId = "#intl_pop_" + asin;
	    
		if (intlPopover.shouldAutocheck) {
		    jQuery("#intl_pop_chk_atc_" + asin).attr('checked','checked');
		}


		jQuery(asinHtmlId).show();
	    
		if (i < asinsToShow.length - 1) {
		    // show the HR for all elements except the last
		    jQuery("#intl_pop_hr_"+asin).show().css('margin','10px auto');
		}
	    }
	}

        // Attach event handler to close button
        jQuery("#intl_pop_body .ap_custom_close,.ap_close").click(function (event) {
            // If they clicked on the single-asin version Add to Order button, we sneakily
            // check the hidden checkbox

            var singleAsinAtcId = 'intl_pop_addToOrder';

            if (jQuery(this).attr("id") == singleAsinAtcId) {
                jQuery("#intl_pop_chk_" + asinsToShow[0]).attr('checked','checked');
            }
            intlPopover.onHide(asinsToShow);
        });

    };

intlPopover.onHide = function(asinsToShow) {
	for (var i=0; i<asinsToShow.length; i++) {
	    var asin = asinsToShow[i];
	    var popoverCheckbox = jQuery("#intl_pop_chk_"+asin);

	    var bbCheckbox = jQuery("#bb_chk_" + asin);
	    
	    if (popoverCheckbox.length > 0 && bbCheckbox.length > 0 && popoverCheckbox.is(':checked')) {
		bbCheckbox.attr('checked', 'checked');
		bbCheckbox.change();
	    }

	}

        if (jQuery("#buyboxDivId [name=submit.add-to-cart]").length ==1) {
        	jQuery("#buyboxDivId [name=submit.add-to-cart]").trigger("click"); //original Detail page
        } else if (jQuery("#addToCart").length ==1) {
        	jQuery("#addToCart").submit();       //DPX DP
        }
}

intlPopover.setupBindings = function() {
    // there is a redesign which may change the buybox DOM
    intlPopover.buttonParent = "#twisterAddToCartOrig";   // original Detail page
    intlPopover.button = intlPopover.buttonParent;
    if (jQuery("#addToCartSpan").length == 1)  {
        intlPopover.buttonParent = "#addToCartSpan";      // updated detail page
        intlPopover.button = intlPopover.buttonParent;
    } else if (jQuery("#addToCartAsShownButtonWrapper").length) {
      intlPopover.buttonParent = "#addToCartAsShownButtonWrapper"; // updated to attach to configurator experience treatment T2
      intlPopover.button = intlPopover.buttonParent;
    } else if (jQuery("#submit\\.add-to-cart").length) {
      intlPopover.buttonParent = "#submit\\.add-to-cart";   // DPX addToCart button
      intlPopover.button = "#add-to-cart-button";	
    }

    jQuery(intlPopover.buttonParent).removeAmazonPopoverTrigger();
    jQuery(intlPopover.button).bind('click', function ( event ) {
	intlPopover.onShow(allAsins, event);
	eventObj = event;
    });

    jQuery('.intl_pop_checkbox').click(function (event) {    
	var checkbox = jQuery(this);
	var asin = checkbox.val();
	var url = "/gp/digital/fiona/ajax/log.html/ref=intl_pop_" + asin + "_" + refTag + ((checkbox.is(':checked')) ? "_chk" : "_uchk");
	jQuery.post( url );
    });
};

   intlPopover.setupBindings();
    


   jQuery(intlPopover.buttonParent).amazonPopoverTrigger({
    title: "Add to your Kindle order",
    localContent: "#intl_pop_body",
    modal: true,
    location: "centered", 
    width: parseInt(jQuery("#intl_pop_body").attr('width'), 10) || 650,
    onShow: function() {
    	eventObj.stopPropagation();  
	    eventObj.preventDefault();
    }       
     });
});
});


</script>

          amznJQ.onReady('jQuery', function() {
            jQuery('.MHRExpandLink').click(function(event){
            event.preventDefault();
	        jQuery(this).hide();

            var parent = jQuery(this).parent();
            var fullText = parent.find(".MHRHead").html() +  parent.find(".MHRRest").html();
            var pxInitialSize = parent.height();
      
            parent.html(fullText);
            var pxTargetSize = parent.height();
            parent.height(pxInitialSize);
            parent.animate({height: pxTargetSize + 'px'}, 400, function() {parent.css("height", "auto")});
          });
        });
      

/* customer-reviews */

amznJQ.onReady('jQuery', function() {
  var voteAjaxDefaultBeforeSendReviews = function(buttonAnchor, buttonContainer, messageContainer) {
    messageContainer.html('Sending feedback...'); 
    buttonContainer.hide(); 
    messageContainer.show();
  };
  var voteAjaxDefaultSuccessReviews = function(aData, aStatus, buttonAnchor, buttonContainer, messageContainer, isNoButton, inappUrl) { 
    if (aData.redirect == 1) {
      return window.location.href=buttonAnchor.children[0].href;
    }
    if (aData.error == 1) {
      jQuery(buttonContainer.children()[0]).html('Sorry, we failed to record your vote. Please try again');
      messageContainer.hide();
      buttonContainer.show();
    } else {
      messageContainer.html('Thank you for your feedback.');
      if (isNoButton == 1) {
        messageContainer.append('<span class="black gl5">If this review is inappropriate, <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/voting/cast/Reviews/2115/R3KVJS35XJVP8B/Inappropriate/1?ie=UTF8&target=&token=267E63BBFCE89F45203A17336B0C9B710B6A6480&voteAnchorName=R3KVJS35XJVP8B.2115.Inappropriate.Reviews&voteSessionID=000-0000000-0000000" class="noTextDecoration" style="color: #039;" >please let us know.</a></span>');
        messageContainer.find('a').attr('href', inappUrl);
      }
      messageContainer.addClass('green');
    }
  };
  var voteAjaxDefaultErrorReviews = function(aStatus, aError, buttonAnchor, buttonContainer, messageContainer) { 
    jQuery(buttonContainer.children()[0]).html('Sorry, we failed to record your vote. Please try again');
    messageContainer.hide();
    buttonContainer.show();
  };

  jQuery('.votingButtonReviews').each(function(){
    jQuery(this).unbind('click.vote.Reviews');
    jQuery(this).bind('click.vote.Reviews', function(){
      var buttonAnchor = this;
      var buttonContainer = jQuery(this).parent();
      var messageContainer = jQuery(buttonContainer).next('.votingMessage');
      // Grab the url for the inapp url and then change change the url to it when rendered
      var inappUrl = messageContainer.children()[0].href;
      var isNoButton = jQuery(this).hasClass('noButton');
      jQuery.ajax({
        type: 'GET',
        dataType: 'json',
        ajaxTimeout: 10000,
        cache: false,
        beforeSend: function(){ 
          voteAjaxDefaultBeforeSendReviews(buttonAnchor, buttonContainer, messageContainer); 
        },
        success: function(data, textStatus){ 
          voteAjaxDefaultSuccessReviews(data, textStatus, buttonAnchor, buttonContainer, messageContainer, isNoButton, inappUrl); 
        },
        error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
          voteAjaxDefaultErrorReviews(textStatus, errorThrown, buttonAnchor, buttonContainer, messageContainer);
        },
        url: buttonAnchor.children[0].href+'&type=json'
      });
      return false;
    });
  });
});
